              I've already got one here, so what I'm going to do--
             </a>

             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="4000" starttime="31000">
              So first of all, you have to lay out some components,
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="3000" starttime="35000">
              so it actually looks like chat, you know?
             </a>

              So I have here my text history and also text message field,
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="3000" starttime="42000">
              and a sending button.
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="3000" starttime="45000">
              So when you go to the source code, it looks like this,
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="3000" starttime="48000">
              and we can see that it's a server
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="4000" starttime="51000">
              which is pointing to stratus.adobe.com with RTMFP protocol.
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="4000" starttime="55000">
              And then, we also include our developer key here--
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="1000" starttime="59000">
              like that.
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="3000" starttime="60000">
              So first of all, we have to connect to the server,
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="6000" starttime="63000">
              so this is what we do by defining function connect,
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="5000" starttime="69000">
              and also initializing netConnection, so we create a variable netConnection
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="5000" starttime="74000">
              of type NetConnection, obviously,
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="4000" starttime="79000">
              and we just initialize it, new NetConnection--
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="3000" starttime="83000">
              like this.
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="3000" starttime="86000">
              And now, we just register the Listener for it,
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="3000" starttime="89000">
              NET_STATUS event, like this:
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="4000" starttime="92000">
              (NetStatusEvent.NET_STATUS,netStatus);
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="2000" starttime="96000">
              We have to create a function as well:
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="6000" starttime="98000">
              function netStatus(event:NetStatusEvent):void{
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="6000" starttime="104000">
              and we just include a NetStatus event like this.
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="6000" starttime="110000">
              So finally, we are in NetStatus, and we just write a message we get from the NetStatus,
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="3000" starttime="116000">
              so it's (event.info.code);
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="8000" starttime="119000">
              And the next thing we are actually going to do--a connection to the server, so like this:
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="4000" starttime="127000">
              netConnection.connect
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="6000" starttime="131000">
              and we include (SERVER+DEVKEY); like this.
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="8000" starttime="137000">
              So once we are in NetStatus, we just switch the (event.info.code);
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="10000" starttime="145000">
              and in case it's "NetConnection.Connect.Success":
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="4000" starttime="155000">
              which means we are successfully connected to the Stratus service.
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="3000" starttime="159000">
              We just set up the group like this:
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="3000" starttime="162000">
              setupGroup(); and we also break it.
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="3000" starttime="165000">
              So now we have to add the setupGroup function
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="7000" starttime="168000">
              setupGroup():void{
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="2000" starttime="175000">
              Well, we do two things.
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="3000" starttime="177000">
              First of all, we have to define so-called Group Specifier,
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="4000" starttime="180000">
              which defines what you can actually do with the NetGroup.
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="13000" starttime="184000">
              It's type GroupSpecifier, and we initialize it
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="9000" starttime="197000">
              and we include a group name, like this--so "myGroup/g0);
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="3000" starttime="206000">
              And so we also enable the posting,
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="2000" starttime="209000">
              so posting means that you can actually broadcast message
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="3000" starttime="211000">
              to the participants of the group.
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="3000" starttime="214000">
              So we change it to true: postingEnabled = true
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="3000" starttime="217000">
              and we also enable server channel: serverChannelEnabled = true
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="4000" starttime="220000">
              which means that this essential thing for the communication
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="3000" starttime="224000">
              which enables you to work with the server actually.
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="6000" starttime="227000">
              So the next thing we have to do here is define the actual NetGroup
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="6000" starttime="233000">
              of type NetGroup.
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="7000" starttime="239000">
              Now, again, we initialize it,
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="3000" starttime="246000">
              we connect to netGroup netConnection,
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="7000" starttime="249000">
              and we also pass this spec: groupspecWithAuthorizations());
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="4000" starttime="256000">
              There is also a difference between groupspecWithAuthorizations
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="3000" starttime="260000">
              and WithoutAuthorizations, but you don't have to care about this now--
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="4000" starttime="263000">
              it's all about the security of the groups.
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="3000" starttime="267000">
              And we also register the Listener:
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="3000" starttime="270000">
              addEventListener(NetStatusEvent.NET_STATUS,netStatus);
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="2000" starttime="273000">
              like this.
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="3000" starttime="275000">
              That's pretty much it--now we have to do 2 more functions.
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="3000" starttime="278000">
              One of them is going to send a message to the group
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="3000" starttime="281000">
              and one of them is going to receive the message from the group.
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="2000" starttime="284000">
              So how does it work?
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="4000" starttime="286000">
              First of all, we create function called sendMessage,
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="5000" starttime="290000">
              and we'll pass a string to it like this: (txt:String):void{
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="3000" starttime="295000">
              We have to cross-track to the message object:
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="6000" starttime="298000">
              so we just write: var message:Object = new Object();
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="6000" starttime="304000">
              And message object should contain some information about a text
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="5000" starttime="310000">
              and also some information about a user
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="9000" starttime="315000">
              so we pass userName, which is going to be the txtUser.text;
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="5000" starttime="324000">
              and also some sort of id, so we can actually--
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="5000" starttime="329000">
              we would like to connect or send a direct message to the sender
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="3000" starttime="334000">
              who actually broadcasted his message, so if you want to do that, you can include
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="6000" starttime="337000">
              sender id, and it's going to be netConnection.nearID
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="5000" starttime="343000">
              You can also convert this nearID to groupID, like that, which is pretty useful.
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="10000" starttime="348000">
              netGroup.convertPeerIDToGroupAddress(netConnection.nearID);
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="2000" starttime="358000">
              to group address--like this.
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="3000" starttime="360000">
              So finally, we are pretty much done.
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="5000" starttime="363000">
              We just post the message to the new group,
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="6000" starttime="368000">
              and now we are going to receive it, so we define function
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="6000" starttime="374000">
              receiveMessage
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="5000" starttime="380000">
              it's going to handle that (message:Object):void{
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="8000" starttime="385000">
              And finally, we just writeText(message userName+= txt+"n/";
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="4000" starttime="393000">
              Yeah, so you can see that this is what we have already defined,
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="5000" starttime="397000">
              and "+message.text); like that.
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="3000" starttime="402000">
              Also, the one thing--you actually broadcast the message to the group,
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="6000" starttime="405000">
              but you don't receive it, so what you have to do here is receiveMessage(message);
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="2000" starttime="411000">
              like that.
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="1000" starttime="413000">
              Okay, we are pretty much done.
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="5000" starttime="414000">
              The last thing we have to do here is actually receive the message,
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="6000" starttime="419000">
              and you actually receive the message in NetStatus.
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="7000" starttime="425000">
              So this is what happens in a case when NetGroup posting gets notified:
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="3000" starttime="432000">
              "NetGroup.Posting.Notify":
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="3000" starttime="435000">
              Something like that--yeah.
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="7000" starttime="438000">
              So "NetGroup.Posting.Notify" and we pass to the receiveMessage function,
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="6000" starttime="445000">
              we pass this (event.info.message); variable like that.
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="5000" starttime="451000">
              Also, the last thing to make it more useful and more prettier to the application itself,
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="7000" starttime="456000">
              you can also handle "NetGroup.Connect. Success" as well,
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="9000" starttime="463000">
              and for instance-- like switch connected to true,
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="1000" starttime="472000">
              like that.
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="5000" starttime="473000">
              So now it's actually connected with this button here,
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="4000" starttime="478000">
              so it got enabled when the connected is true--by default, it's false.
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="4000" starttime="482000">
              So at the final state, we are going to test the application and see if it works,
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="3000" starttime="486000">
              so we go and just press the Run button,
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="3000" starttime="489000">
              and we write a message
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="5000" starttime="492000">
              and we hit Send, and we can see now that it's received,
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="6000" starttime="497000">
              so we can do from the outer window--so the way back--it works as well.
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="3000" starttime="503000">
              Okay, and that's pretty much it, so I hope it was easy to use
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="4000" starttime="506000">
              and I'm actually looking forward to seeing more and more applications
             </a>
             <a class="caption" duration="2000" starttime="510000">
              using peer-to-peer in the future.
